class sequence extends $mol_room {
  note_index(next?: number) { return next ?? -1 }

  onend() {
    let next = this.note_index() + 1
    if (next >= this.notes.length) next = -1

    this.note_index( next )
  }

  @ $mol_mem
  playing() {
    const index = this.note_index()
    if (index === -1) return false
    const note = this.notes[index]

    this.output()

    return true
  }
}

    @ $mol_mem
    protected node_start() {
      const started = $mol_wire_probe(() => this.node())?.started
      if (started === true) this.node_raw(null)

      const node = this.node()
      node.start(this.start_at())
      node.started = true

      return null
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    protected node_stop() {
      if (this.stop_at() <= this.start_at()) return null

      const node = this.node()
      node.stop(this.stop_at())

      return null
    }


    @ $mol_mem
    override output() {
      this.node_start()
      this.node_stop()
      return super.output()
    }

    @ $mol_mem
    start_at(when?: number) {
      const next = when + this.time_cut()

      const instruments = []
      for (const clip of this.clips()) {
        const instrument = this.instrument(clip.id)

        instrument.start_at(next + clip.start_at)
        instruments.push(instrument)
      }
      this.input(instruments)

      return next
    }

> The octave of a note is indicated by a number following the pitch name. Octave 1 is the octave starting at middle C (C4), and going up through the note B4. One octave higher than middle C is octave 2, and octave 0 is one octave lower than middle C. The octave below 0 is -1, which is indicated like this: c-1.
